Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 5, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











The fastest way to earn a couple of byes is to win them at a Grand Prix Trial. A total of 44 players won their respective pods yesterday and we're glad to share all of them for your kind perusal.


Seeing how this was the first individual *Dominaria* Premier Event in the world, maybe you'll learn a thing or two the next time you tackle a Sealed Deck! [Skittering Surveyor](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Skittering+Surveyor) is enabling three or four-colored decks, while the most played (and splashed) removal spells are [Eviscerate](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Eviscerate) and [Shivan Fire](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Shivan+Fire).


Potent bombs also played a pivotal role in crushing your opponents, so having cards like [Verdant Force](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Verdant+Force), [Shalai, Voice of Plenty](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Shalai%2C+Voice+of+Plenty), or even [Darigaaz Reincarnated](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Darigaaz+Reincarnated) meant a great deal. Oh yes, having both [Karn, Scion of Urza](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Karn%2C+Scion+of+Urza) and [Teferi, Hero of Dominaria](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Teferi%2C+Hero+of+Dominaria) in the same deck is also pretty epic, or should I say, legendary!







#### Shao Xiaogang
